The `stringformat` filter is decorated with `@register.filter(is_safe=True)`. More importantly, `is_safe=True` on a filter means its output won't be escaped by autoescape when the input is safe.\n\nActually, let me think about this more carefully. In Django templates:\n- `is_safe=True` means the filter doesn't change the \"safeness\" of the value in a way that introduces unsafe characters. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01Y2EgChQgKXQA6H3UKd44AK","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I see some important tests:\n1. `test_render_quoted` - Tests that HTML special characters in a value are properly escaped.\n2. `test_attrs_safestring` - Tests that `mark_safe()` values are NOT escaped (they pass through as-is).\n\nThese tests pass. But notice that `test_render_quoted` is testing the **value** field, not the **attrs** field. There's no test for special characters in the **attrs** values.\n\nNow let me think about what the task is asking for. The bug says:\n> \"When a form field widget specifies custom HTML attributes through a `build_attrs` call, certain attribute values are not properly escaped when they contain special characters like quotes or ampersands.\"\n \nSo the issue is with attributes like `data-label=\"Value with \"quotes\"\"` - when the attribute value contains quotes, they're not being escaped properly. I need to look at how the `attrs.html` template actually renders these attributes to understand where the escaping is failing.\n\nLooking at both the Django and Jinja2 template versions, I see they're iterating through the widget attributes and building the HTML. The key question is whether auto-escaping in Jinja2 would escape the quotes inside the attribute value, and if so, whether that would break the attribute syntax itself by turning the `\"` delimiters into `&#34;`.\n\nActually, that's the right behavior—auto-escaping should convert quotes to their HTML entity equivalents, which is the proper way to include quotes in attribute values.
